        isOpen: false,

        livewire: null,

        close: function () {
            this.isOpen = false

            this.$refs.modalContainer.dispatchEvent(
                new CustomEvent('modal-closed', { id: 'database-notifications' }),
            )
        },

        open: function () {
            this.$nextTick(() => {
                this.isOpen = true

                
                this.$refs.modalContainer.dispatchEvent(
                    new CustomEvent('modal-opened', { id: 'database-notifications' }),
                )
            })
        },
    }" x-on:close-modal.window="if ($event.detail.id === 'database-notifications') close()" x-on:open-modal.window="if ($event.detail.id === 'database-notifications') open()" x-trap.noscroll="isOpen" x-bind:class="{
